id="siteNotice"><!-- CentralNotice --></div><div class="mw-indicators mw-body-content">\n</div>\n<h1 class="firstHeading" id="firstHeading" lang="en">Timeline of Solar System exploration</h1> <div class="mw-body-content" id="bodyContent">\n<div class="noprint" id="siteSub">From Wikipedia, the free encyclopedia</div> <div id="contentSub"><span class="mw-redirectedfrom">&#160;&#160;(Redirected from <a class="mw-redirect" href="/w/index.php?title=Timeline_of_planetary_exploration&amp;redirect=no" title="Timeline of planetary exploration">Timeline of planetary exploration</a>)</span></div>\n<div id="jump-to-nav"></div> <a class="mw-jump-link" href="#mw-head">Jump to navigation</a>\n<a class="mw-jump-link" href="#p-search">Jump to search</a>\n<div class="mw-content-ltr" dir="ltr" id="mw-content-text" lang="en"><div class="mw-parser-output"><p class="mw-empty-elt">\n</p>\n<div class="thumb tright"><div class="thumbinner" style="width:222px;"><a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Timeline_of_Solar_System_exploration.jpg"><img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="3839" data-file-width="3500" decoding="async" height="241" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Timeline_of_Solar_System_exploration.jpg/220px-Timeline_of_Solar_System_exploration.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Timeline_of_Solar_System_exploration.jpg/330px-Timeline_of_Solar_System_exploration.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/6/6b/Timeline_of_Solar_System_exploration.jpg/440px-Timeline_of_Solar_System_exploration.jpg 2x" width="220"/></a> <div class="thumbcaption"><div class="magnify"><a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Timeline_of_Solar_System_exploration.jpg" title="Enlarge"></a></div>Charted timeline of Solar System exploration, as of December 2014</div></div></div>\n<p>This is a <b>timeline of Solar System exploration</b> ordered by date of <a href="/wiki/Spacecraft" title="Spacecraft">spacecraft</a> launch. It includes:\n</p>\n<ul><li>All spacecraft that have left Earth orbit for the purposes of <a href="/wiki/Discovery_and_exploration_of_the_Solar_System" title="Discovery and exploration of the Solar System">Solar System exploration</a> (or were launched with that intention but failed), including <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Lunar_probe" title="Lunar probe">lunar probes</a>.</li>\n<li>A small number of pioneering or notable Earth-orbiting craft.</li></ul>\n<p>It does <i>not</i> include:\n</p>\n<ul><li>The great majority of Earth-orbiting satellites.</li>\n<li><a href="/wiki/Space_probe" title="Space probe">Space probes</a> leaving Earth orbit that are not concerned with Solar System exploration (such as <a href="/wiki/Space_telescope" title="Space telescope">space telescopes</a> targeted at distant galaxies, <a href="/wiki/Cosmic_background_radiation" title="Cosmic background radiation">cosmic background radiation</a> observatories, and so on).</li>\n<li>Probes that failed at launch.</li></ul>\n<p>The dates listed are launch dates, but the achievements noted may have occurred some time later&#8212;in some cases, a considerable time later (for example, <i><a href="/wiki/Voyager_2" title="Voyager 2">Voyager 2</a></i>, launched 20 August 1977, did not reach Neptune until 1989).\n</p><p>Missions in <i>italics</i> are unfinished, i.e. have not yet been designated as successes or failures. Some unitalicised missions are nevertheless still operational, some in mission extension phases.\n</p>\n<div class="toc" id="toc"><input class="toctogglecheckbox" id="toctogglecheckbox" role="button"
